 Tabrez Ansari was attacked by the mob on 17 June

 People beat Tabarez as a thief
 is ghatana kaa ek video bhi saamne aayaa tha jisamen log use dhamkaate hue dikh rahe the or jai shri ram kaa naaraa lagane ke liye kah rahe the

 is maamle main doctoron kaa kahana he ki tabrej ne kabhi sir main dard kii shikaayat nahin kii thi

 lekin doctoron dwaara maut kii vajah saamne aane ke baad postmortem report or police ke ravaiye par sawaal khadaa hota he, jisaki chautarafa aalochana bhi hui thi

 chot bhi ek vajah he
 'J Amalorpavanathan, a doctor in Chennai, said that a fracture could lead to a heart attack

 History of Shahjahanpur Talking about the political background of Shahjahanpur Lok Sabha seat, this parliamentary seat came into existence during the 1962 Lok Sabha elections
 shuruaati teen chunaav main congress ne jeet hasil kii, lekin 1977 main sarkaar virdohi lahar main congress ko yahaan se bhi haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa or jeet janata dal ke khate main gai
 However, after 3 years, when the elections were held in the country again in 1980, the Congress returned here with a victory
 1980 ke baad 1984 main bhi congress ke tikat par jitendra prasad ne jeet hasil kii
 In the 90s, during the era of Ram wave, BJP rapidly emerged in UP and emerged as a big party
 1989 or 1991 ke chunaav main bijepi ne jeet hasil kii
 However, the Samajwadi Party won the 1996 election and gave a blow to the BJP
 2 saal baad 1998 main bijepi phir yahaan se jeet gai, lekin 1999 main chunaav main congress ke jitendra prasad vaapasi karne main kaamyaab ho gaye
 After his death in 2001, his son Jitin Prasad won elections from this seat in the 2004 general election
 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaav main jeet samaajawaadee party ke khate main gai, lekin 2014 ke chunaav main bhartiya janata party ne phir is seat par jeet hasil kii
